=
google_ads;




if(google_ads.length
!=
0)
{








apply_ad_config(google_ads.length);









render_ads(true,
window['ad_config_top']);









if(window['backfillParam'])
{












window['backfillParam']['pl_rnum']
=
google_ads.length;












window['backfillParam']['pl_time']
=
Date.now()
-
afc_ad_start_time;








}




}
}

function
apply_ad_config(num)
{
window['ad_config_top']
=
Math.min(2,
num);
window['ad_config_bot']
=
Math.min(2,
num);
}

google_ad_client
=
'ca-aj-cat';
google_ad_channel
=
'cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN';
google_ad_output
=
'js';
google_max_num_ads
=
'4';
google_ad_type
=
'text';
google_image_size
=
'';
google_num_ads_recieved=
'';
google_language
=
'';
google_country
=
'';
google_encoding
=
'utf8';
google_safe
=
'medium';
google_adtest
=
'off';
google_ad_section
=
'default';
google_page_url
=
'';
google_hints
=
'George_Harrison';
google_kw
=
'';
google_kw_type
=
'broad';


var
backfillParam
=
{




pl_rqnum
:
google_max_num_ads,




pl_hints
:
google_hints,




pl_rp
:
"false",




pl_kw
:
google_kw,




pl_cl
:
google_ad_client,




pl_ch
:
google_ad_channel,




pl_hex
:
"#FDFEEE",




pl_type
:
"afc",




pl_clksp
:
"none"};

var
word_arr
;

var
word_arr_len
;


function
highlightQuery(input_str)
{

var
queryTokenArray
=
"george,harrison,_,";


var
tok_arr
=
queryTokenArray.split(",");

for(tok_arr_idx=0;
tok_arr_idx
<
tok_arr.length-1;
tok_arr_idx
++)
{

if(isCombinationWord(tok_arr[tok_arr_idx])){
word_arr
=
tok_arr[tok_arr_idx].split("-");
word_arr_len
=
word_arr.length;
first_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(word_arr[0],0);

if(first_pos
!=-1)
{
input_str
=
highlightCombinationWords(input_str,first_pos);
}
}
else
{
first_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(tok_arr[tok_arr_idx],0);
if(first_pos
!=
-1
&&
tok_arr[tok_arr_idx].length
>
0)
{
input_str
=
highlightSimpleWords(input_str,tok_arr[tok_arr_idx],first_pos);
}
}
}
return
input_str;
}

function
isCombinationWord(word){
if(word.indexOf("-")
!=
-1){
return
true;
}
else
{
return
false;
}
}


function
isAlpha(ch)
{
if
(ch
!=
null
&&
ch.match(/^[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/)){
return
true;
}
return
false;
}

function
isQueryinInput(firstindex,
input_str,
j){
for(i=firstindex;
i<
input_str.length
;
++i)
{
var
currindex
=
i;

if(!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(i)))
{
if(firstindex
==
currindex)

{
firstindex++;
}
else
{
if(word_arr[j]
!=
input_str.substring(firstindex,currindex).toLowerCase())
return
-1;
if
(j
==
word_arr_len-1)
return
currindex;
else
return
isQueryinInput(currindex+1,input_str,++j);
}
}
}

if(j
<
word_arr_len)
{
if(word_arr[j]
!=
input_str.substring(firstindex,currindex+1).toLowerCase())
return
-1;
}

return
(currindex
+
1)
;
}


function

highlightCombinationWords(input_str,first_pos)
{
exactmatch
=
isQueryinInput(first_pos+word_arr[0].length,input_str,1)
;
if(exactmatch
!=-1
)

{
bold_str
=
"<b>"
+
input_str.substring(first_pos,exactmatch)
+
"</b>";
input_str
=
input_str.substring(0,first_pos)
+
bold_str
+
input_str.substring(exactmatch);
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(word_arr[0],exactmatch+7);
while(next_pos
!=
-1)
{
return
highlightCombinationWords(input_str,next_pos);
}
}
return
input_str;
}


function

highlightSimpleWords(input_str,token,
first_pos)
{
var
end_pos
=
first_pos
+
token.length;
if(!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(end_pos))
&&
!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(first_pos-1))){
bold_str
=
"<b>"
+
input_str.substring(first_pos,end_pos)
+
"</b>";
input_str
=
input_str.substring(0,first_pos)
+
bold_str
+
input_str.substring(end_pos);
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(token,end_pos+7);
}
else
{
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(token,end_pos);
}

while(next_pos
!=
-1)
{
return
highlightSimpleWords(input_str,token,next_pos);
}
return
input_str;
}</script>

<p><b>George
Harrison</b>,<sup
id="cite_ref-3"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-3"><span>[</span>nb
1<span>]</span></a></sup>
<span
style="font-size:100%"><a
href="/wiki/Member_of_The_Most_Excellent_Order_of_the_British_Empire?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Member
of
The
Most
Excellent
Order
of
the
British
Empire"
class="mw-redirect">MBE</a></span>
(25
February
1943&nbsp;–
29
November
2001)
was
an
English
musician,
singer
and
songwriter
who
achieved
international
fame
as
the
lead
guitarist
of
<a
href="/wiki/The_Beatles?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Beatles">the
Beatles</a>.
Although
<a
href="/wiki/John_Lennon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
Lennon">John
Lennon</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paul
McCartney">Paul
McCartney</a>
were
the
band's
primary
songwriters,
most
of
their
albums
included
at
least
one
Harrison
composition,
including
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/While_My_Guitar_Gently_Weeps?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="While
My
Guitar
Gently
Weeps">While
My
Guitar
Gently
Weeps</a>&quot;,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Here_Comes_the_Sun?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Here
Comes
the
Sun">Here
Comes
the
Sun</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Something?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Something">Something</a>&quot;,
which
became
the
Beatles'
second-most-<a
href="/wiki/Cover_version?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cover
version">covered</a>
song.</p>








<p>Harrison's
earliest
musical
influences
included
<a
href="/wiki/Big_Bill_Broonzy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Big
Bill
Broonzy">Big
Bill
Broonzy</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/George_Formby?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="George
Formby">George
Formby</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Django_Reinhardt?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Django
Reinhardt">Django
Reinhardt</a>;
<a
href="/wiki/Chet_Atkins?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Chet
Atkins">Chet
Atkins</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Chuck_Berry?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Chuck
Berry">Chuck
Berry</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Ry_Cooder?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ry
Cooder">Ry
Cooder</a>
were
significant
later
influences.
By
1965
he
had
begun
to
lead
the
Beatles
into
<a
href="/wiki/Folk_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Folk
rock">folk
rock</a>
through
his
interest
in
<a
href="/wiki/The_Byrds?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Byrds">the
Byrds</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Bob_Dylan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bob
Dylan">Bob
Dylan</a>,
and
towards
<a
href="/wiki/Indian_classical_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Indian
classical
music">Indian
classical
music</a>
through
his
use
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Sitar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sitar">sitar</a>
on
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Norwegian_Wood_(This_Bird_Has_Flown)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Norwegian
Wood
(This
Bird
Has
Flown)">Norwegian
Wood
(This
Bird
Has
Flown)</a>&quot;.
He
developed
an
interest
in
the
<a
href="/wiki/International_Society_for_Krishna_Consciousness?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="International
Society
for
Krishna
Consciousness">Hare
Krishna
movement</a>
and
became
an
admirer
of
<a
href="/wiki/Culture_of_India?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Culture
of
India">Indian
culture</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Mysticism?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mysticism">mysticism</a>,
introducing
them
to
the
other
members
of
the
Beatles
and
their
Western
audience
by
incorporating
Indian
instrumentation
in
their
music.
After
<a
href="/wiki/Break-up_of_the_Beatles?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Break-up
of
the
Beatles">the
band's
break-up</a>
in
1970,
Harrison
released
the
triple
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/All_Things_Must_Pass?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="All
Things
Must
Pass">All
Things
Must
Pass</a></i>,
from
which
two
hit
singles
originated.
He
also
organized
the
1971
<a
href="/wiki/The_Concert_for_Bangladesh?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Concert
for
Bangladesh">Concert
for
Bangladesh</a>
with
<a
href="/wiki/Ravi_Shankar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ravi
Shankar">Ravi
Shankar</a>,
a
precursor
for
later
<a
href="/wiki/Benefit_concert?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Benefit
concert">benefit
concerts</a>
such
as
<a
href="/wiki/Live_Aid?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
Aid">Live
Aid</a>.
Harrison
was
a
music
and
film
producer
as
well
as
a
musician;
he
founded
<a
href="/wiki/Dark_Horse_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dark
Horse
Records">Dark
Horse
Records</a>
in
1974
and
co-founded
<a
href="/wiki/HandMade_Films?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="HandMade
Films">HandMade
Films</a>
in
1978.</p>








<p>Harrison
released
several
best-selling
singles
and
albums
as
a
solo
performer,
and
in
1988
co-founded
the
<a
href="/wiki/RIAA_certification?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="RIAA
certification">platinum-selling</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Supergroup_(music)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Supergroup
(music)">supergroup</a>
the
<a
href="/wiki/Traveling_Wilburys?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Traveling
Wilburys">Traveling
Wilburys</a>.
A
prolific
recording
artist,
he
was
featured
as
a
guest
guitarist
on
tracks
by
<a
href="/wiki/Badfinger?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Badfinger">Badfinger</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Ronnie_Wood?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ronnie
Wood">Ronnie
Wood</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Billy_Preston?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billy
Preston">Billy
Preston</a>,
and
collaborated
on
songs
and
music
with
Bob
Dylan,
<a
href="/wiki/Eric_Clapton?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Eric
Clapton">Eric
Clapton</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Tom_Petty?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tom
Petty">Tom
Petty</a>,
among
others.
<i><a
href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rolling
Stone">Rolling
Stone</a></i>
magazine
ranked
him
number
11
in
their
list
of
the
&quot;100
Greatest
Guitarists
of
All
Time&quot;.</p>








<p>Harrison's
first
marriage,
to
<a
href="/wiki/Pattie_Boyd?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pattie
Boyd">Pattie
Boyd</a>,
ended
in
divorce
in
1977.
The
following
year
he
married
<a
href="/wiki/Olivia_Harrison?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Olivia
Harrison">Olivia
Trinidad
Arias</a>,
with
whom
he
had
one
son,
<a
href="/wiki/Dhani_Harrison?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dhani
Harrison">Dhani</a>.
Harrison
died
in
2001,
aged
58,
from
lung
cancer.
He
was
cremated
and
his
ashes
were
scattered
in
the
<a
href="/wiki/Ganges?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ganges">Ganges</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Yamuna?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yamuna">Yamuna</a>
rivers
in
India,
in
a
private
ceremony
according
to
<a
href="/wiki/Ganges_in_Hinduism?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ganges
in
Hinduism">Hindu
tradition</a>.
He
left
almost
&pound;100
million
in
his
will.</p>

style="overflow:hidden;height:;">

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="1943.E2.80.9357:_early_years">1943–57:
early
years</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=George_Harrison&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1"
title="Edit
section:
1943–57:
early
years">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<div
class="rellink">








Further
information:









<a
href="/wiki/The_Quarrymen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Quarrymen">The
Quarrymen</a>







</div>








<div
class="thumb
tright">









<div
class="thumbinner"
style="width:172px;">









<a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:12ArnoldGrove.JPG"
target="_blank"
class="image"><img
alt="Exterior
of
a
red
brick
building.
Visible
are
a
black
door
with
a
small
window
just
above
it,
two
larger
windows
to
the
left
of
the
door,
one
above
the
other,
and
a
flowerpot
between
the
door
and
the
lower
larger
window"
src="http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/12ArnoldGrove.JPG/170px-12ArnoldGrove.JPG"
width="170"
height="227"
class="thumbimage"
srcset="http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/12ArnoldGrove.JPG/255px-12ArnoldGrove.JPG
1.5x,
http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/12ArnoldGrove.JPG/340px-12ArnoldGrove.JPG
2x"
/></a>










<div
class="thumbcaption">











<div
class="magnify">











<a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:12ArnoldGrove.JPG"
target="_blank"
class="internal"
title="Enlarge"><img
src="http://sp.ask.com/sh/i/wiki/magnify-clip.png"
width="15"
height="11"
alt=""
/></a>










</div>
Harrison's
first
home
and
place
of
birth
–











<a
href="/wiki/12_Arnold_Grove?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="12
Arnold
Grove">12
Arnold
Grove</a>









</div>









</div>








</div>








<p>Born
in
<a
href="/wiki/Liverpool?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a>,
Lancashire,
England,
on
25
February
1943,
Harrison
was
the
youngest
of
four
children
of
Harold
Hargreaves
Harrison
and
his
wife
Louise
(n&eacute;e
French).<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEMiles20016_4-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEMiles20016-4"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
had
one
sister,
Louise,
and
two
brothers,
Harry
and
Peter.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEHarry2000492_5-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEHarry2000492-5"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup>
His
mother
was
a
shop
assistant
from
a
<a
href="/wiki/Catholic_Church?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Catholic
Church">Catholic</a>
family
with
Irish
roots,
and
his
father
was
a
bus
conductor
who
had
worked
as
a
ship's
steward
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/White_Star_Line?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="White
Star
Line">White
Star
Line</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-6"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup>
His
future
wife,
the
model
Pattie
Boyd,
described
Harrison's
parents
as
&quot;quite
short
and
very
Liverpudlian&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBoyd200782_7-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBoyd200782-7"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup>
According
to
Boyd,
Harrison's
mother
was
particularly
supportive:
&quot;All
she
wanted
for
her
children
is
that
they
should
be
happy,
and
she
recognized
that
nothing
made
George
quite
as
happy
as
making
music.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBoyd200782_7-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBoyd200782-7"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup>
An
enthusiastic
music
fan,
she
was
known
among
friends
for
her
loud
singing
voice,
which
at
times
startled
visitors
by
rattling
the
Harrisons'
windows.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTESpitz2005120_8-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTESpitz2005120-8"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup>
While
pregnant
with
George,
she
often
listened
to
the
weekly
broadcast
<i>Radio
India</i>.
Harrison's
biographer
Joshua
Greene
wrote,
&quot;Every
Sunday
she
tuned
in
to
mystical
sounds
evoked
by
sitars
and
<a
href="/wiki/Tabla?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tabla">tablas</a>,
hoping
that
the
exotic
music
would
bring
peace
and
calm
to
the
baby
in
the
womb.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEGreene20062_9-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEGreene20062-9"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Harrison
was
born
and
lived
the
first
six
years
of
his
life
at
<a
href="/wiki/12_Arnold_Grove?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="12
Arnold
Grove">12
Arnold
Grove</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Wavertree?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wavertree">Wavertree</a>,
Liverpool,
in
a
<a
href="/wiki/Terraced_house?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Terraced
house">terraced
house</a>
in
a
<a
href="/wiki/Cul-de-sac?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cul-de-sac">cul-de-sac</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEHarrison200220.E2.80.9321_10-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEHarrison200220.E2.80.9321-10"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
home
had
an
outdoor
toilet
and
its
only
heat
came
from
a
single
coal
fire.
In
1949
the
family
were
offered
a
<a
href="/wiki/Council_house?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Council
house">council
house</a>
and
moved
to
25
Upton
Green,
<a
href="/wiki/Speke?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Speke">Speke</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEMiles20017_11-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEMiles20017-11"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
1948,
at
the
age
of
five,
Harrison
enrolled
at
Dovedale
Primary
School.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEInglis2010xiii_12-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEInglis2010xiii-12"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
passed
his
<a
href="/wiki/11-plus?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="11-plus"
class="mw-redirect">11-plus</a>
examination
and
attended
the
prestigious
<a
href="/wiki/Liverpool_Institute_High_School_for_Boys?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Liverpool
Institute
High
School
for
Boys">Liverpool
Institute</a>
from
1954
to
1959.<sup
id="cite_ref-13"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-13"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Harrison's
earliest
musical
influences
included
<a
href="/wiki/George_Formby?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="George
Formby">George
Formby</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Cab_Calloway?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cab
Calloway">Cab
Calloway</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Django_Reinhardt?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Django
Reinhardt">Django
Reinhardt</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Hoagy_Carmichael?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hoagy
Carmichael">Hoagy
Carmichael</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Big_Bill_Broonzy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Big
Bill
Broonzy">Big
Bill
Broonzy</a>.
In
early
1956
he
had
an
epiphany:
while
riding
his
bicycle,
he
heard
<a
href="/wiki/Elvis_Presley?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Elvis
Presley">Elvis
Presley</a>'s
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Heartbreak_Hotel?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Heartbreak
Hotel">Heartbreak
Hotel</a>&quot;
playing
from
a
nearby
house,
and
the
song
piqued
his
interest
in
<a
href="/wiki/Rock_and_roll?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rock
and
roll">rock
and
roll</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-14"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-14"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
often
sat
at
the
back
of
the
class
drawing
guitars
in
his
schoolbooks,
and
later
commented,
&quot;I
was
totally
into
guitars&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTELange20016_15-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTELange20016-15"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Although
apprehensive
about
his
son's
interest
in
pursuing
a
music
career,
in
late
1956
Harrison's
father
bought
him
a
Dutch
Egmond
flat
top
acoustic
guitar.<sup
id="cite_ref-16"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-16"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
friend
of
his
father's
taught
Harrison
how
to
play
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Whispering_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Whispering
(song)">Whispering</a>&quot;,
&quot;Sweet
Sue&quot;,
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Dinah_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dinah
(song)">Dinah</a>&quot;,
and
inspired
by
the
music
of
<a
href="/wiki/Lonnie_Donegan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lonnie
Donegan">Lonnie
Donegan</a>,
Harrison
formed
a
skiffle
group
called
the
Rebels
with
his
brother
Peter
and
a
friend,
<a
href="/wiki/Arthur_Kelly_(actor)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Arthur
Kelly
(actor)">Arthur
Kelly</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-17"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-17"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
the
bus
to
school
Harrison
met
<a
href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paul
McCartney">Paul
McCartney</a>,
who
became
a
member
of
<a
href="/wiki/John_Lennon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
Lennon">John
Lennon</a>'s
band
<a
href="/wiki/The_Quarrymen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Quarrymen">the
Quarrymen</a>,
and
the
pair
bonded
over
their
shared
love
of
music.<sup
id="cite_ref-18"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-18"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<div
style="clear:right;"></div>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="1958.E2.80.9370:_the_Beatles">1958–70:
the
Beatles</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=George_Harrison&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2"
title="Edit
section:
1958–70:
the
Beatles">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<div
class="rellink
relarticle
mainarticle">








Main
article:









<a

onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Beatles">The
Beatles</a>







</div>

tleft">

<div
class="magnify">

</div>
Harrison
at
a
press
conference
in
the
Netherlands
in
1964









</div>









</div>








</div>








<p>In
March
1958
Harrison
auditioned
for
the
Quarrymen
at
<a
href="/wiki/Rory_Storm?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rory
Storm">Rory
Storm</a>'s
Morgue
Skiffle
Club,
playing
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Guitar_Boogie_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Guitar
Boogie
(song)">Guitar
Boogie
Shuffle</a>&quot;,
but
Lennon
felt
that
Harrison,
then
14,
was
too
young
to
join
the
band.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTESpitz2005125.E2.80.93126_19-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTESpitz2005125.E2.80.93126-19"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup>
During
a
second
meeting,
arranged
by
McCartney,
he
performed
the
lead
guitar
part
for
the
instrumental
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Raunchy_(instrumental)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Raunchy
(instrumental)">Raunchy</a>&quot;
on
the
upper
deck
of
a
Liverpool
bus.<sup
id="cite_ref-20"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-20"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup>
Soon
afterwards
he
began
socializing
with
the
group,
filling
in
on
guitar
as
needed,<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEDavies200944.E2.80.9345_21-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEDavies200944.E2.80.9345-21"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
by
the
time
he
turned
15
they
had
accepted
him
as
a
member.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTELewisohn199213_22-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTELewisohn199213-22"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup>
Although
his
father
wanted
him
to
continue
his
education,
Harrison
left
school
at
16
and
worked
for
several
months
as
an
apprentice
electrician
at
<a
href="/wiki/Blacklers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blacklers">Blacklers</a>,
a
local
department
store.<sup
id="cite_ref-23"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-23"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
1960
<a
href="/wiki/Allan_Williams?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Allan
Williams">Allan
Williams</a>
arranged
for
the
band,
now
calling
themselves
the
Beatles,
to
play
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Kaiserkeller?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kaiserkeller">Kaiserkeller</a>
club
in
<a
href="/wiki/Hamburg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hamburg">Hamburg</a>,
owned
by
<a
href="/wiki/Bruno_Koschmider?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bruno
Koschmider">Bruno
Koschmider</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEMiles199757.E2.80.9358_24-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEMiles199757.E2.80.9358-24"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
impromptu
musical
education
Harrison
received
while
playing
long
hours
with
the
Beatles,
as
well
as
the
guitar
lessons
he
took
from
<a
href="/wiki/Tony_Sheridan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tony
Sheridan">Tony
Sheridan</a>
while
they
briefly
served
as
his
backing
group,
laid
the
foundations
of
his
sound
and
of
his
quiet,
professional
role
within
the
group;
he
was
later
known
as
&quot;the
quiet
Beatle&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-25"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-25"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
band's
first
residency
in
Hamburg
ended
prematurely
when
Harrison
was
deported
for
being
too
young
to
work
in
nightclubs.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEMiles200127_26-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEMiles200127-26"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup>
When
<a
href="/wiki/Brian_Epstein?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brian
Epstein">Brian
Epstein</a>
became
their
manager
in
December
1961,
he
polished
their
image
and
secured
them
a
recording
contract
with
<a
href="/wiki/EMI?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="EMI">EMI</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-27"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-27"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
group's
first
single,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Love_Me_Do?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Love
Me
Do">Love
Me
Do</a>&quot;,
peaked
at
number
seventeen
on
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Record_Retailer?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Record
Retailer">Record
Retailer</a></i>
chart,
and
by
the
time
their
debut
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Please_Please_Me?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Please
Please
Me">Please
Please
Me</a></i>,
was
released
in
early
1963,
<a
href="/wiki/Beatlemania?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Beatlemania">Beatlemania</a>
had
arrived.<sup
id="cite_ref-28"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup>
Their
second
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/With_the_Beatles?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="With
the
Beatles">With
the
Beatles</a></i>
(1963),
included
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Don%27t_Bother_Me?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Don't
Bother
Me">Don't
Bother
Me</a>&quot;,
Harrison's
first
solo
writing
credit.<sup
id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEEverett2001193_29-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEEverett2001193-29"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<div
class="thumb
tright">









<div
class="thumbinner"
style="width:222px;">









<a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:The_Beatles_in_America.JPG"
target="_blank"
class="image"><img
alt="Black-and-white
picture
of
four
young
men
outdoors
in
front
of
a
staircase,
surrounded
by
a
large
assembled
crowd.
All
four
are
waving
to
the
crowd."
src="http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/The_Beatles_in_America.JPG/220px-The_Beatles_in_America.JPG"
width="220"
height="155"
class="thumbimage"
